               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 美國數學解題團
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 數學是利用符號語言研究數量、結構、變化以及空間[等概念的一門學科，從某種角度看屬於形式科學的一種。數學透過抽象化和邏輯推理的使用，由計數、計算、量度和對物體形狀及運動的觀察而產生。數學家們拓展這些概念，為了公式化新的猜想以及從選定的公理及定義中建立起嚴謹推導出的定理。廣告是不允許的。此團是給住在美國的數學解題團。因為每一個不同地區/國家的教學方式、解題難度、認知上差異太多。請諒解！ 謝謝。 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Welcome to SoCal Engineers What's the purpose of SoCal Engineers Facebook page ? The ultimate goal is to connect engineers in SoCal together. Who are the members? Engineers, student engineers, faculty engineers, &amp; professionals working with engineers. Can I add more members? Sure we encourage everyone to add the engineers they know. What can be discussed at this page? Engineering related topics, new technologies used in engineering, new codes and regulations, &amp; work related advises. Can I post job openings in SoCal engineers ? Yes definitely we encourage everyone to post engineering position and internships. How can I help and be an active member? Currently we are looking for someone to work with students to help them build resumes and score internships.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Oculus Quest
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Oculus Quest is a new standard of standalone AR VR headset that will feature two motion controllers for hand tracking. Devices of this type are the future of Mixed Reality XR devices. I’m convinced that standalone AR VR devices that give you hand presence in mobile VR are the future of VR. Oculus Quest is a mobile all in one VR headset, no phone or computer required, 6 degrees of freedom for both hands and your head. This class of device will let you walk around in VR (as you move in the real world) and you get to have your hands in VR so you can reach out touch virtual objects and move them around. These types of devices will eventually allow users to stream cinematic quality holographic lightfield based VR games rendered on GPU clouds that will look better than what can be rendered on a local desktop computer machine. This group follows Google’s anti-harassment policy, in other words be excellent to each other and to the group, keep posts on topic, if anyone gives you trouble do not engage with them just report their comment to the admin, and you can take a screenshot and message it to me at micah@vrma.work https://www.google.com/events/policy/anti-harassmentpolicy.html Update for May 7th 2019: This group is rated G for all audiences. If you mention adult content, even jokingly, you may get booted from all the groups I admin including this one, and all your posts from this week may get deleted at the same time (that's an admin tool that we have) This group is about the Oculus Quest first and foremost, about standalone VR secondarily, about gaming in VR after that, and there may be a small minority of people who are not expecting to see or hear references to adult content, a small minority of people who may not feel safe discussing that, so for them, for the few people, it's considered off topic for this group. Please be polite towards all people. Update July 8th 2019 Observe the group rules, read the group description, and don't engage in conversations where the group topic is not appropriate for ALL audiences. If there was a conversation about an inappropriate topic "Exhibit A" and you said "haha" in response, that warrants being muted because you engaged in and elevated a conversation that was about an inappropriate topic, even if your comment in isolation would not be considered an issue. If you see someone starting an inappropriate topic, don't even react with a like or a laugh, because that is also elevating and engaging with an inappropriate topic and your action means that more people will see it which is why the mute, remove, or ban buttons will come into play. Don't react, report.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 FREE Solving Math Problems
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 If you need a little help in high school mathematics and lower division college math or have some time to help someone in high school mathematics and lower division college math you are more than welcome to join this group. Here are some guidelines for the group: 1. Topics may include Algebra, Statistics, Probability, Coordinate Geometry, Precalculus, Differential &amp; Integral Calculus, Multivariable Calculus, Linear Algebra (Matrix Theory) and Differential Equations. 2. Use only English to post and comment. 3. Post only math questions of appropriate level in which you are having difficulty or need some explanation. 4. Be polite and respectful to other members. 6. Do not post any kind of advertisement or link to any websites in any post or comment. 9. Do not post a question that has been posted recently. 11. Try not to post questions by taking a picture from the textbook. Type it out as best as you can. Avoid misunderstanding by appropriate use of parentheses. 12. If you must post an image because it is a Geometry problem, it better be your own image, not something you picked up in the web, and add your own description of the problem. 14. Do not engage in exchanging personal information in the comments. Give other members their privacy. 15. Follow the rules in the group. Tags: Mathematics · Education

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Nature
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The words nature and natural are used for all the things that are normally not made by humans. Things like weather, organisms, landforms, celestial bodies, stones, animals plants, wind, rain, earthquakes, flood and much more are part of Nature. Nature provided us many things including living and as well as non-living things. Let us see what makes living things different from non-living things. 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 🌿Living things (Biotic part) 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ (i) They breathe air. (ii) They need food and water. (iii) They grow. (iv) Most of them move on their own (v) They can reproduce. (vi) They can feel. 🌴🥀🌱 🐆🐎🐕 🦅🐦🐧🦈🐜🕷️🐞 👉 Plants, animals, birds, fish, bacteria, mashroom, fungi, and human beings are natural things. 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 🌦️Non-living things (Abiotic part). 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ The abiotic part of nature consist of all things, that were not made by man and are not living. (i) they do not breathe. (ii) they do not need food and water. (iii) they do not grow. (iv) they cannot move on their own. (v) they do not reproduce. (vi) they cannot feel. 🏔️⛰️🏜️🏞️🗺️🗾🏝️🌄🌌🚞🌉🚆🌋🗻 👉 Water, light, wind, soil, humidity, minerals, gases, mountains, rocks, rain, cloud etc 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 👉You can post /share any thing in the world that you find interesting in nature. You are allowed to post/share images of Nature like animals/sea animals, butterflies, birds/sea birds, sea shores, oceans, beaches, deserts, lacks, rocks, landscapes, gardens, trees, mountains , vegetables, fruits and flowers etcetera. 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 📚Group Rules 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 🌿 Please post pictures, only drawn from the camera's eyes. 🌿 No Nudity, No porn. Nothing offensive. No loveable /offensive comments. Stickers, Stickers in comments, pictures in comments and text on images are not allowed. 🌿 Please do comment to posts not personal, don't use vulger language in comments over in any picture. 🌿 'Advertising posts, 'Comments containing adverts', 'Religious posts', Good morning /evening /night posts are not allowed. 🌿 Please deal one another with positive manners/respect. Group forum is not for chatting. 🌿 Links of pages/groups, youtube, Facebook, Instagram etcetera are not allowed. 🌿 3D pictures, Ticktalk, voumbla, youtube images and videos are not allowed. 🌿 Please don't allowed more then 07 pictures daily for any member. 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ 🔴 Failures of rules, will be immediately out 🆘and block without any notification. ✔️ 〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️ Thanks you all, pl feel free and enjoy the nature! Admin Muhammad Raza 
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Teaching Behavior Analysis
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is the Teaching Behavior Analysis SIG of the Association for Behavior Analysis International. The network is intended for sharing of ideas and updates in conjunction with the TBA website and listserv. Anyone who teaches others to change behavior is welcome. This includes educators, professionals, parents, and other interested parties! Note that this is not an autism-specific group - posts about anything related to behaviorism and Applied Behavior Analysis are welcome. Posts not specifically related to behavior analysis (including general autism information) will be deleted. Spam posts (defined as either posts for items not related to behavior analysis OR more than three posts for the same product in one week) and advertisements for non-behavioral products will be removed, and users will be permanently banned. Advertisements for trainings and services are welcome, but solicitation of funds (e.g., GoFundMe campaigns) will be deleted. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">7,696 位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">0 篇新帖</span></span>

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Research Empowering Protection Website coming soon. VISION The vision of Shark Ecology And Sealife Society is to expand the knowledge of young people, the general public, and to share research knowledge and exchange methodologies with other researchers about sharks and the marine environment they survive in and to be actively involved in conservation, education, protection, and to assist and participate in shark research projects worldwide using traditional methods and the latest technology. To encourage people young and old to actively participate in the much needed research and conservation of sharks and the marine environment GROUP. Views expressed in this group do not necessarily reflect those of the Page Administrator(s) or owners. All members are encouraged to post comments photographs, personal experiences, tell us not only about the bad tell us about the good you see being done and the good work others are doing. Please do report issues concerning the conservation sharks of any species. As a group we need to work together to conserve sharks and the marine environment, we can make a difference for the good and change misinformed perceptions. Group started by active shark researchers Remember “Sometimes failing to prove the expected gives you the solution” RULES Posts that will get you banned, there may be other reasons but they will include the following:- Totally disregarding the rules of the page continually. Posting about or promoting illegal activities and action. Racial / political / cultural slurs / threats of violence and hostility, excessive swearing and profanity. Trolls, creating argument situations or posts just to get a reaction and cause disruption. Posting annoying or objectionable material, pornography, spam, adverts selling travel / sunglasses / or suchlike, images that have nothing to do with group subject general objectionable material, abuse of admins. (if you have problem, report it to the admins) GENERAL GUIDELINES Keep posts on forum topics. If using a general photo from the internet or news story please try to credit the original photographer or news source. Duplicate / double posts, we will delete the newest version and leave the original. All posts wanting support (financial) / fundraising / sale of any item / travel / advertising of businesses, petitions etc must have admin permission No posts promoting other companies or products of any kind, especially companies / pages etc you are involved in If you do not like what another member posts please just block them. Respect other people’s views, they may not be yours but please respect everyone. Remember, healthy adult debate is good, arguments and personal attacks are bad. If in doubt about anything ASK AN ADMIN.

                 Bio Hacker Tribe
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is a support group for biohackers. We are here to share any and all biological, psychological, social, and/or spiritual "hacks" for the human experience. Group guidelines : 😀 All posts should be either a question or information about biohacking the biological, emotional, social, and/ or spiritual. 🙏 Please be respectful of all points of view. 👁‍🗨 Please use the search bar at the top of the group to search past posts, before you post on a topic. 🚫 Product or page promotion is forbidden - links can be shared for informational purposes only. Food / diet posts that have a little to do with bio hacking are not allowed (there are other groups for that) ----------------------------------- ❌Safety warning/disclaimer ❌ ----------------------------------- Many experienced bio hackers in this group like to share about their personal experiments – Many of these experiments use substances or medications that are not approved to be used in this fashion by Western allopathic medicine. It should be understood that these people assume all risk for doing these experiments with themselves . You should always consult a health professional, before doing any of these experiments, or do them at your own risk. This is a bio hacking group, so please be open-minded and respectful. --------------------- ⚡️What is bio hacking – ⚡️ Bio hacking is about optimizing one's own personal physiology , by researching (and understanding) peer reviewed scientific papers, and devising n=1 experiments, utilizing a thorough understanding of the scientific method, and gathering results. What biohacking is not – Taking on faith what the traditional medical establishment, any one person, or advertisement promotes; only "researching" blog posts on the Internet (although they can often be a good starting point for a pub med search)
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Forbidden Archaeology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Authority may be a hint as to what the truth is, but is not the source of information. As long as it's possible, we should disregard authority whenever the observations disagree with it. -- Richard P. Feynman Forbidden archaeology is archaeology that is unacceptable to the mainstream archaeological mind. Here is a place to discuss those cases that rarely see the light of day or that are deemed impossible. Our prime directive is to educate and be educated in ska safe and peaceful environment and to facilitate civil discussion and debate. To Those Who Request to Join Us: If you do not have a photo of yourself on your timeline, your request will be denied. If you do not answer the questions your request will be denied as well. We screen our member so that everyone can enjoy the group. We strive to maintain a peaceful group where all of our members are treated with respect and dignity. Please help us do this by answering the prerequisite questions and obeying the rules. Thank you, The Admins and Moderators p.s.: Lets keep this group totally free from current politics and related issues. Thanks!

                 SHPE Region 2
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 SHPE Region 2 is the oldest and greatest region of the Society of Hispanic Professional Engineers. SHPE was founded in 1974 by engineers in Los Angeles, and Southern California has remained the roots of SHPE ever since. Mission SHPE changes lives by empowering the Hispanic community to realize their fullest potential and impacts the world through STEM awareness, access, support and development. Vision SHPE's vision is a world where Hispanics are highly valued and influential as the leading innovators, scientists, mathematicians and engineers. "Network with like-minded, ambitious people. Make a difference in your community. Become a leader."

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ancient and Medieval History and Archaeology Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A place to share and discuss medieval and ancient history and archaeology. Here is a list of some group guidelines and rules. Firstly, we do not expect everyone in here to be a scholar or to be able to post only scholarly sources. We are not a peer reviewed journal. HOWEVER, we do want to maintain some level of integrity to our topics here. Controversial topics or alternative theories may be okay. However, if your topic is controversial or alternative, then it is important to share from an authoritative source. It doesn't have to be journal or university, but Smithsonian, Archaeology Mag, NatGeo, etc, would be more reliable than some whack-a-doo alternative theory site. Which brings me to the next important point. It has become important to emphasize yet again... NO ALIENS. No ifs ands or buts. There are groups for that. This is not it. Other than that, we are very laid back moderators. Just common sense and courtesy, be respectful and keep the vibe positive. Please read these guidelines: - We do strive to stay on topic and will remove any spam such as advertisements for unrelated things and ban spammy users. - This is a place for intellectual discussion and a haven from heated political arguments. So please keep discussion in a historical context and leave modern politics out of it. - Aggressive, nasty, rude speech to other group members is cause for removal. Here's a list of community standards and participation guidelines from The Guardian which apply to and are followed by this group. https://www.theguardian.com/community-standards
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Botany Everyday
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Botany Every Day group focuses in the tradition of Frank Cook on doing a little botany every day. It mainly hosts cross postings from an online botany class facilitated by marc williams and others using the book Botany in a Day as a primary text at www.botanyeveryday.com Related events that are of ethnobotanical interest are posted as well. Any contributions to this work energetically, commentarily, or financially are greatly appreciated. Thanks, marc DISCLAIMER: Use of Information marc williams has carefully selected and enjoyed edible plants both wild and cultivated for many years. Foragers often need numerous quality references and personal knowledge gained from studying plant materials through classroom and "hands on" training in order to harvest safely. Please seek professional advice before using any plants if you are at all unsure. When in doubt leave it out. marc williams or anyone associated with the development or distribution of material at www.botanyeveryday.com or this facebook group assume no liability for any actions taken in viewing, reading, or using any information provided herein. Please use caution when collecting, preparing, and utilizing any plants. Information Accuracy marc williams as the main developer of Botany Every Day makes every effort to provide and maintain accurate, complete, useable, and timely information. However, the data and information herein are provided with the understanding that they are not guaranteed to be correct or complete. Conclusions drawn from or actions undertaken on the basis of, such data and information are the sole responsibility of the user. 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Audio Engineering Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was originally founded as the Audio Engineering Society group. But now we are just the Audio Engineering Group. Essentially, this Facebook Group is an industry trade group for those who are professional audio engineers, and for audio production students formally training for a career in audio engineering. This group has many professionals that are happy to share their experience and knowledge. Please be considerate of their time. While we encourage the growth of each individual’s knowledge, if an answer to a question can be found via user documentation and/or a simple web search, please read over that content first before bringing that subject to this forum. To ensure unrelated posts and spam do not appear on the group, please note the POSTING GUIDELINES below. (Feel free to send us any comments on these guidelines!) WE ENCOURAGE POSTS THAT ARE: 1- TEXT-based questions, comments, discussion points. 2- Helpful, educational, and directly relevant to Professional Audio Production 3- Videos and/or media posts that offer "significant professional, educational merit" THE FOLLOWING TYPES OF POSTS ARE NOT ACCEPTABLE AND WILL BE REMOVED: 1- blatant self-promotion, (or even unblatant self-promotion) 2- any type of advertising or advertorial links 3- any post not on-point to the forum 4- any post showing aggressive/rude behavior or language 5- any type of SPAM (obviously!) 6- any questions on cracked software, using cracked s/w, or where/how to get it 7- jokes or comical posts (they are fun, but are just noise to some - pun intended) 8- videos or cross posts from other forums/blogs (unless a specific question or discussion point accompanies it) or fail to meet qualifications set above 9- posts regarding politics and religion 10- posts promoting specific performance acts, recordings and similar without the discussion of specific audio engineering subjects 11- posts badmouthing/bashing others, especially engineers and/or producers 12- posts intended to seek out potential customers for your products or services (unless someone specifically asks for those recommendations) 13- posts from Bots or other automatic spamming devices REPEATED OFFENSES TO THE ABOVE WILL RESULT IN THE REMOVAL OF THAT GROUP MEMBER
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 All Things Algebra® Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created specifically for those who use the All Things Algebra Math 6, Math 7, Pre-Algebra, Algebra 1, Geometry, Algebra 2, or PreCalculus curriculum resources. This creates a community for teachers to share how they implement All Things Algebra resources. This also allows me to more efficiently announce updates, and get some feedback too! Some guidelines: 1- Due to copyright risks, please do not share or ask fellow teachers for resources. This includes asking members to share files through email or private messaging. 2- Do not post advertisements for outside resources, businesses, and/or products. 3- Do not ask group members for followers, votes, donations, etc. 4- If you find an error in an answer key, please send it directly to me at allthingsalgebra@gmail.com rather than posting in the group. (This is kinda a biggie, I may miss it if you post it here, but I will definitely see it in email!) 5- Feel free to tag me, however, I may not see or be able to respond to every tag. If you have a specific question that can not be answered by fellow group members, please email me at allthingsalgebra@gmail.com. Thank you!

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Avid Pro Tools Users Group. Group Admins: Fahim Ahmed Paulash, Marco Bernardo, Dave Phillips, Simon Nakra Please read the rules after joining and also when in doubt on the type of posts allowed. THE RULES: What this Forum is intended for: • Posts about Pro Tools and associated hardware where help, advice and guidance is required. Also sharing your Pro Tools set ups and sharing stories. • Treating everyone with respect. • General discussions about Avid and Pro Tools. • Avid update notifications. What we DO NOT allow on this Forum (posts will be deleted): • Self-Promotional posts. There are plenty of other groups where you can share your mixes, tutorials, brand and competitions. • Abusive language and/or personal insults towards fellow members and admins. • The discussion of cracked software. • Spamming. • Off topic posts (nothing to do with Pro Tools or Avid). Persistent posting of what we DO NOT allow will result in the member being removed from this Forum and blocked from re-joining. If you feel like having a rant about Pro Tools and/or Avid, please feel free to join and post here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/protoolsforumthetwilightmoan/ If you are interested in Pro Tools Collaboration and working with other members, please feel free to join and post here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/ProtoolsCloudCollaboration/ If you have something to sell that relates to Avid products, please feel free to join and post here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/ProtoolsForumSecondhandClassifieds/ Enjoy using this Forum and please feel free to post and reach out for help, advice and guidance. We have a fantastic community of members who are always happy to help out when required. Many thanks!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Megalodon Shark Teeth And Fossils
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Megalodon shark teeth and fossils was created to be an informative group, to help teach about and share fossil finds. This group is dedicated to sharing discussion, research, photographs, and questions regarding the fossils. Members here are helpful with the sharing of ideas, we have a wide range of friends that will be happy to share knowledge. We love to help other members learn, and show off our finds along the way. If you would like a fossil ID please provide several pictures and collecting information/state found. Pictures should be clear and not blurry, and not on a black background. Natural light is best . *************Group rules************** 1. We are not here to give up our fossil collecting sites so please don’t ask! 2. No soliciting of members for donations. If you are solicited for fossils/ harassed make one of the admin aware of the problem via private message. Save message and forward to DEBRA POWELL FIRST then an admin. 3. Be polite and just tell them you're not interested! 4. Selling is not permitted in this group. We are not here to advance your online business. 5. Off topic posts will be deleted. 6. No profanity, respect your other members. 7. Posts should be of fossils that can spark interesting and educational discussion. 8. ***Absolutely no artifacts*** should be posted or discussed. This group is for fossils only. ****************************************** Face book group! The bone yard trading post: https://www.facebook.com/groups/816909588327244/ Fossil Invertebrates: https://www.facebook.com/groups/673080969453333/ Matrix hunters: https://www.facebook.com/groups/738219916213892/ Florida fossil collecting permit: http://www.flmnh.ufl.edu/natsci/vertpaleo/permitapplication.htm Canoe rental: http://www.canoeoutpost.com/peace/default.asp This is your group, members here have done a outstanding job in making it such a success. I thank you. Paleo hugs

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Endangered Plants of California
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Post Reminder: always, please, include a habitat (site) photograph of the location where you observe a CNPS rare/threatened/endangered plants This group concentrates on endangered, threatened or rare plants of California – 2293 plants of most recent count. Please restrict posts to plants included on the CNPS Inventory (http://www.rareplants.cnps.org/). This group in intended to serve as a social arm of the overall CNPS Inventory, facilitating quick reporting of information. With perhaps 1,000 botanists in California engaged in rare plant field surveys, it is hoped that limitations restricting information flow are removed via this group. For other California native plant sightings, horticultural observations, and miscellany please post to California Native Plant Society or for non-natives to California Invasive Plants. Plants not on the CNPS Inventory are not posted here. Posts of new discoveries are encouraged. Also favored are photographs of the habitat setting in which CNPS rare plants are recorded, and details about other ecological setting information. 1. please include Taxon Name, Family, CNPS List status (i.e. Funastrum crispum (Benth.) Schltr. Apocynaceae, CNPS List 2B.2) on all submittals 2. for all posted records, include the date of the photograph, and geographic details: County, location, and by posting here you affirm that your record will be submitted to the CNDDB. Where appropriate, include GPS coordinates (assuming protection of the location does not require anonymity), voucher information is encoured. 3. For known CNDDB Element Occurrences, include the EO#. 4. If your posting is intended to propose CNPS Inventory status for a non-listed taxon, say so explicitly. Affirm that you will provide sufficient review documentation such that your plant can be considered for inclusion on the CNPS Inventory. 5. CBR – Considered but Rejected plants are welcomed. 6. This the inaugural pinned post guidelines will, initially, be revised, and input is welcomed. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Girls in Tech (GIT) is a global non-profit that works to put an end to gender inequality in high-tech industries and startups. We do that by educating and empowering women who are passionate about technology. As a result, we offer everything from coding courses to bootcamps to hackathons and startup competitions no matter age or profession. It is Girls in Tech’s mission to support women with the access and community they need to succeed in tech. GIT was founded in 2007 and headquartered in San Francisco. The Girls in Tech global community is 60 chapters strong with an impact of more than 100,000 members in 36 countries. As a result, events and programming in each chapter vary to fit the unique needs of each community. https://girlsintech.org/ [Be sure to Like our Page: http://www.facebook.com/GirlsInTech!}

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Clinical Psychology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Clinical psychology is a broad branch of scientific psychology that focuses on diagnosing and treating mental, emotional, and behavioral disorders. However, the aim of this group is NOT to provide emotional support or counseling to individuals suffering from emotional problems. If you are experiencing emotional problems please contact a clinical psychologist in your area. The aim of this group is to help students of psychology in improving their understanding of psychology and providing conceptual clarity in different areas of the discipline. We are here to share knowledge of academic psychology both with students and the general audience to improve their theoretical knowledge and practical experience so that psychology could help them in their academics and daily lives. 
                </div>
               </div>

           <div class="_8sz1 _8sz5 _8szd _8szj" id="u_0_41">

             <a class="_8ulx" href="/groups/256522333305/">
              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Maths Puzzles
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group where people can post maths puzzles (hard or easy) as a challenge to everyone else. Some rules: Post any problem you want under the following guidelines 1) If it is a self made problem, say it is.. If it isn't a self made problem, quote the source 2) You should have a solution available for your problem 3) If you don't have a solution to your problem, then explicitly state it before the wording of the problem. 4) Please do NOT post links and/or pictures (unless accompanying a geometry problem or such) 5) Please do NOT post homework problems 6) Under NO circumstances should Spam be posted. 7) Discussions within threads are encouraged 8 ) Isolated results/solutions are discouraged, and people should [attempt to] show full methods/techniques/argumentation together with the results/solutions they give 9) Please refrain from posting multiple problems in quick successions. 10) Only maths problems/puzzles should be posted (not physics) 11) Do not post philosophical views 12) Do NOT post ambiguous mathematical problems e.g. 12/2(6-7+4)*2 13) Do not post FALSE mathematical problems that use "tricks" to solve them 14) Do NOT post ambiguous maths questions (How do you... etc..).. Please only post maths puzzles/problems... If you want the answer to general maths questions either google them or go to another maths page 15) All puzzles/problems must be in English We are NOT a HELP site, do not post any general mathematical problems/theory that you need help with.. Please go to https://www.facebook.com/yourmathguru for that. Any post that breaks these rules will be deleted. Any spam will be deleted and the poster will be banned.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Applied Behavior Analysis
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This closed group is a private forum exclusively for ABA Professionals actively certified and registered in good standing by the Behaviour Analyst Certification Board (BACB) to promote the science and dissemination of Applied Behaviour Analysis. The rules outlined below are non-negotiable. All membership requests are reviewed by group administrators. Professionals of related disciplines will be accepted at the discretion of the group administrators. We acknowledge each other as equals with respect to ability, age, appearance, class, ethnicity, gender, neurotype, religion, sex, sexual orientation, and other identity groups. We provide useful comments, affirmative to the principles of ABA, and respectful when in disagreement. Criticisms and negative experiences of ABA should be worded in a professional and respectful manner. We expect that what is said here, stays here (distribution of screenshots of group conversations will result in removal from the group). Posts can be saved for future reference by clicking the three dots at the top right of the post and selecting “save post.” We base our discussions on the science, principles, and ethics of Applied Behaviour Analysis and the Behaviour Analyst Certification Board (BACB). Discussions will focus on evidence-based therapies, applications, treatments, and interventions. •Any and all comments and posts are reviewed by the group administrators and can be deleted at administrator discretion. Posts that will be deleted immediately include extremist, derogatory, libelous, factually inaccurate, and/or slanderous behaviour and/or verbiage. Any and all comments/posts must align with the BACB’s Professional and Ethical Compliance Code (PECC). •Personal attacks directed at members of the group, including group administrators, will not be tolerated. Members are expected to engage with one another and group administrators respectfully; refraining from name-calling and foul language. The offending member can be removed immediately without notice. •Business solicitations and CEU offerings are not permitted outside of weekly designated threads. Product, service, and job opportunity posts are not allowed. •Repeated posts and comments (spam) are not allowed and will be removed. •If a member is unsure if their desired post will violate any of the group rules, they are encouraged to send a private message to group administrators. •If a member would like to report or discuss a member, post, or any other matter they are encouraged to send a private message to the group administrators. *Members may not block group administrators. 
                </div>

                 Visual Math
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hi Teachers! 👉Please answer all questions and agree with group rules when requesting to join👈 This is a group of math educators helping each other reach kids who learn best through visuals and who may be juuust a little bit (or a whole lot) afraid of math. All kids can be successful in math with the right supports. That’s what this group is for. What thIs group is about: Sharing ideas and strategies for reaching and teaching kids in our classrooms. Math and teaching memes and jokes to keep us laughing are also welcome! What this group is not about: Homework help. Please search YouTube for help with your personal assignments. There are lots of math teaching resources (many free) and ideas on my blog scaffoldedmath.com. I hope it becomes a helpful resource for you! As teachers, we all have so much on our plates. Let’s make this group a place to support and encourage each other. Thank you for being here! -Shana McKay Scaffolded Math and Science

                 Botanical Wanderings - California
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The original purpose of this group was to coordinate botanical trips in California with a focus on native plants. That is complicated given current circumstances. As use of the group evolves, people are using this group to share what they have seen on their own trips. Please share your California wildflower photos, along with info on where you have visited. If you are going on a plant hike and would like to have others join you or know of a botanical event coming up, post the details and invite people along. This group is open to all levels of experience and will hopefully serve as a means of bringing plant lovers together so we can all learn from each other.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Electrical Power, Electrical Circuits and Electrical Wiring (IDEH)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Industrial Development and Environmental Health (IDEH) is an informal discussion and research facilitation organization that promotes activities needed for advancements in health, environmental health, environment, industrial development, agriculture, energy and water resources. Currently most of the discussions are based on low-cost communication tools such Facebook, Google circle and Researchgate with the possibility having a web-based communications in the future. The empowerment of children, adults and the aging from all walks of life are a priority where possible. IDEH relies on volunteer based support in order to assist with activities in areas associated with the matters mentioned in order to serve a growing population. The activities and communications will remain impartial and transparent where possible, and this is done in order to build capacity of all members and non-members alike in the areas mentioned, especially focusing on occupational safety and environmental health aspects associated with the following: +Agriculture and food +Natural Resources +Technology and Engineering +Administration and Law +Industry +Health +Labour +Education +Transport +Archaeological Sites and Culture Preservation +Infrastructure List of IDEH groups .. Industrial Development and Environmental Health (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/IDEH.Main.Group/ Natural Resources (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/227516467434435/ Wetland Ecology &amp; Marine Ecosystems (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/743143405705564/ Geothermal Energy, Geophysics &amp; Contaminant Hydrogeology (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/530739490372734/ Infrastructure &amp; Urban Development (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/1400283106907587/ Earth Dynanmics (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/596320197109947/ IDEH Central &amp; South America https://www.facebook.com/groups/586944721399084/ Air &amp; Water Quality (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/586944721399084/ Solid &amp; Hazardous Waste, and Water &amp; Wastewater Treatment (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/216719518523371/ Rail Transportation &amp; Networks (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/530202513760438/ Home Gardening, Organic Farming &amp; Composting (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/IDEH.Organic.Farming/ Non-communicable Diseases (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/227505764117653/ Infection Control &amp; Infectious Diseases (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/466035840190735/ Food &amp; Drug Safety (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/795892847105740/ Economics &amp; Development (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/664238203614007/ Geography and Geographical Information Systems (IDEH) https://www.facebook.com/groups/344902435657114/

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Society for Humanistic Psychology, Division 32
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This Facebook Group is developed, maintained, and moderated by the Society for Humanistic Psychology (Division 32 of the American Psychological Association). The group is primarily developed for paying members of the Society for Humanistic Psychology as a membership benefit; however, individuals are allowed to join the Facebook group without being a member of the Society for Humanistic Psychology. Individuals must be a member of the Society for Humanistic Psychology to have full participation privileges. All posts are moderated and only members are allowed to post. Anyone is allowed to comment as long as the comments are relevant and consistent with the guidelines and rules for participation developed by the Society for Humanistic Psychology and the American Psychological Association. Information on membership and how to join is available at http://www.apadivisions.org/division-32/membership/index.aspx. Individuals new to the Facebook group interested in being active participants should review the participation guidelines prior to participation. These can be found under the files section and include 1) Division 32 Listserv Welcome with Rules, 2) APA Short and Long Form Rules, and 3) SHP Facebook Posting Policy. We ask all participants in this group to be cognizant that the moderators of this group are current or prior board members of the Society for Humanistic Psychology who are volunteering their time to support the Facebook group. Without their services, this group would not be possible. In order to be respectful of their time and service, please do your best to be familiar with the guidelines if you are going to be an active participant in this group. This is an active Facebook group with many individuals participating. It can, at times, take several hours of volunteer service a week to moderate this group. In order to keep the group sustainable, individual who repeatedly do not follow the rules, including making attempts to posts while not being a member of the Society for Humanistic Psychology, will be removed from the group. It is not possible to moderate all the comments. If you see a comment that is not following the guidelines or is otherwise inappropriate, please contact one of the moderators to ask them to review the comment. If you are posting a request for research participants, you must have obtained IRB or similar approval and information about this should be included in your post in order for it to be approved. Additionally, please note that you still must be a member of the Society for Humanistic Psychology to post this request. A one time announcement of a professional accomplishment, such as having a book, is allowed. However, this should not be an advertisement and repeated posts that are promoting products should be avoided, even if a member of the Society for Humanistic Psychology. 
                </div>

                 Mathematics
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group where you can discuss any mathematical problem. Anyone can post problems and anyone can provide solutions or answers to problems. All posts (questions) however will be approved by an admin or moderator only if in compliant with the group rules. English is the language of communication for this group. Questions could be from various topics such as Algebra, Statistics, Probability, Coordinate Geometry, Precalculus, Differential &amp; Integral Calculus, Multivariable Calculus, Linear Algebra (Matrix Theory), Differential Equations, Trigonometry, 3D Geometry, Vectors, Combinatorics, Binomial Theorem, Mathematical inequalities, Number Theory, Abstract Algebra, Real Analysis, Complex Analysis, Mathematical Modelling, Graph Theory, Topology etc. Check Group Rules for the rules of this group. Violating a group rule will get you blocked from the group.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Archaeology Update
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Archaeology is the study of human activity in the past, primarily through the recovery and analysis of the material culture and environmental data that they have left behind. We are a group of like-minded individuals with a passion for all things related to this field. In order to maintain a level of authenticity and quality, this page will adhere to some specific guidelines. As History and Archaeology are inseparable from and complimentary to each other, History related posts are also welcome within our guidelines. This is a mainstream Archaeology group. NO Pseudo-Archaeology or Alternative History will remain posted. this includes but is not limited to, aliens, giants, angels, demons, ghosts, leprechauns, fairies, goblins, vampires or zombies. NO Biblical, Koranic, Talmudic, Mormonic, Scientological or any other kind of 'holy' book archaeology will remain posted. NO political agenda-forwarding posts will remain posted. NO commercial activities: no false accounts carrying malware pretending to be advertisements for shoes, sunglasses, or computer gadgets will be tolerated here, also general commercial activities will get you removed. NO looted archaeological objects: The illegal excavation and sale of antiquities is completely unacceptable on this page (and beyond). This group will act immediately to remove posters advocating this or attempting to trade in antiquities. While heated intelligent discussions are expected and welcome, NO racial, sexist or homophobic slurs will be tolerated. We have no tolerance for intolerance. An atmosphere of respect and civility must be maintained always. If we take your post down the admin will be happy to discuss it with you. SPAMMERS AND DISRUPTIVE PEOPLE WILL BE BANNED. thanks- admin 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Self-Taught Programmers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Self-Taught Programmers Facebook group is a place for programmers (and aspiring ones) to share their experience, get help, ask questions, and post tech news. Cory Althoff, the author of "The Self-Taught Programmer: The Definitive Guide to Programming Professionally," is the founder and an active participant. The group is ground zero for the Self-Taught Revolution—a movement of people learning to program outside of school. Rules 1. Respect the moderators. 2. Respect other members. 3. Don't ask what the best resource is to learn to program, what IDE everyone uses, or how long it will take you to learn to program. You can find the answers to these questions here: https://github.com/selftaughtprogrammers/popular_discussions. ****** Resources****** Coding List www.codinglist.com The Self-Taught Programmer Book: http://tinyurl.com/y7q8osoa The Self-Taught Programmer Udemy Course: https://www.udemy.com/course/self-taught-programmer/?couponCode=FE5880C9326821C60CFB Self-Taught Blog: https://selftaught.blog Newsletter: http://theselftaughtprogrammer.io ******Social****** Facebook: https://facebook.com/coryalthoff Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/coryalthoff Twitter: https://twitter.com/coryalthoff YouTube: https://www.youtube.com/coryalthofftv GitHub: https://github.com/selftaughtprogrammers If you are new to the group, please start by reading the following post: https://www.facebook.com/groups/selftaughtprogrammers/permalink/393049507725456

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Math Help
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 𝗥𝘂𝗹𝗲𝘀 𝗼𝗳 𝗠𝗮𝘁𝗵’𝘀 𝗛𝗲𝗹𝗽: 𝘔𝘦𝘮𝘣𝘦𝘳𝘴 𝘢𝘳𝘦 𝘳𝘦𝘲𝘶𝘦𝘴𝘵𝘦𝘥 𝘵𝘰 𝘪𝘯𝘧𝘰𝘳𝘮 𝘢𝘥𝘮𝘪𝘯𝘪𝘴𝘵𝘳𝘢𝘵𝘪𝘰𝘯 𝘪𝘧 𝘴𝘶𝘤𝘩 𝘱𝘰𝘴𝘵𝘴 𝘢𝘳𝘦 𝘧𝘰𝘶𝘯𝘥. • All members must show politeness to other members including administration, Impolite posts will be deleted &amp; the member(s) banned. • Posts offering payment for help or asking help for payment is not allowed. Such posts will be deleted &amp; the member banned. • Posts containing sexual material are not tolerated. Such posts will be deleted &amp; the member banned. • All posts must be in English. Posts not in English will be deleted. • If administration assess a post not to be in the interest of the group, it will be deleted. This includes quizzes (guess the number, magic squares &amp; so on) &amp; general advertising. 𝘊𝘰𝘯𝘵𝘪𝘯𝘶𝘢𝘵𝘪𝘰𝘯 𝘰𝘧 𝘱𝘰𝘴𝘵𝘴 𝘰𝘧 𝘵𝘩𝘪𝘴 𝘯𝘢𝘵𝘶𝘳𝘦 𝘸𝘪𝘭𝘭 𝘳𝘦𝘴𝘶𝘭𝘵 𝘪𝘯 𝘢 𝘣𝘢𝘯. • Answers without questions are not allowed and will be deleted. This also pertains to any posts without questions. • No Spam • Only one question per post. Posts containing multiple questions will have the added on questions removed or in some cases , the whole post deleted. • Members multi-posting either the same post repeatedly or many questions for homework use risk having the post or posts deleted altogether pending administational assesment. This is not “the homework group” nor the “John Doe Show” – no member is more important than any other, including posts. • Please remember the main object of this group is for as many members to get as much help from all members. • When agreeing to an answered post, click LIKE instead of posting your answer , repetition serves no purpose. • Photos of problems must be posted with the correct orientation , not side on. Posts containing with side photo’s will be deleted. All photos must not be sideways or upside down. • Broad and General posts will be deleted. Your questions need to be a clear actual problem. No requests for help to "Teach me ___ topic" or broad open ended discussions. • Do not post final answer only. Please provide the work or explanation that follow up your answers. Full explanations help other members learn for themselves and come to an understanding. • No “check my work” posts. We are seeing an abundance of “check my work.” Our goal is for members to help each other solve problems they are having difficulty solving. We are not your teachers and we do not grade your work. • Do NOT delete your questions after they have been answered. • The decision of administration is final.
                </div>

               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The California Mushroom Identification Forum
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is geared towards the identification of wild mushrooms found in California. In your post, please include photographs of both the top and underside, general location, habitat, and any distinctive features not shown in the photograph, (odor, taste, staining, flesh color, etc). Please include the date the mushroom was found. Any off-topic post will be deleted; (mushrooms from outside CA, mycoremediation articles, cultivation, art). **Never eat a mushroom based on an identification from this forum!** Rather, use the suggested name to research it yourself, compare it to your mushroom and then you (and only you) make up your mind to eat it or not. Please also consider uploading your finds to www.inaturalist.org or www.mushroomobserver.org This will give a lasting record of when and where mushrooms are being found, and will greatly improve our knowledge of CA mushrooms. Please keep the discussion respectful. Have fun!
                </div>
               </div>

                 A place for open discussion and debate about issues related to evolution and creationism. While the admins here avoid hard and fast rules (with the exception of the no-blocking rule) and eschew being heavy-handed, we ask that posts and comments always be made with an eye to the twin goals of this page: debate and education. Personal insults--particularly those peppered with foul language--do nothing to promote either goal (other than educating us all in your lack of sophistication and verbal finesse). We'd rather members self-police such posts, but we will remove egregious examples on our own. In that same spirit, blatant attacks on religion or atheism are outside of the ambit of this page and will be removed. Admins will investigate and consult on any complaints by members. Short of blatant merchandising (and sexual solicitations--yes, we've had some), members are not banned without a prior request for an explanation for challenged posts and comments. RULES: Only one: do not block other members. HOWEVER: Original posts are screened, so check this post if something you posted never showed up on this page

                 Creality Official User Group, No matter you use Ender 2, Ender 3, Ender 3 Pro, Ender 3 X, ender3 max, Ender 5, Ender 5 Plus, Ender 5 Pro or CR Series printer(CR-10， CR-10S Pro， CR-X Dual Extruder，CR-10 Max，CR-10 S5，CR-10 V2 ，CR-10S Pro-V2 ，CR-X Pro, etc ), LD-001, LD-002, LD-002R, LD-002H,LD-003, CP-01, Ender 3 V2, Ender 6, CR-6 SE/MAX,CR-5 pro, CR-30, CR-200 etc Creality WIFI box, and Creality cloud app .You can always get massive support or suggestion for your Creality 3d printer. You are welcome to share your unique modesl or some printing tips that is helpful to others member on this group. Currently, It is one of our most active Creality community on Facebook, You won't be feel lonely on our family and we would love to hear your voice if you have any wonderful suggestion or advice. We also host interesting 3d printing contest or Creality product giveaway every month, join our group to get latest news or offer from Creality. For more information, please visit our official website: www.creality3dofficial.com

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ****The basic guidelines of this group.**** 1. Post should be primarily on Jung, psycho-spiritual and creative topics 2. No tolerance to hate speech and their symbols and flags 3. No mockery about religions and other groups 4. No complaint post, if there is an issue on the group, contact an admin 5. No trolling i.e. provocative post and comment even in disguise 6. No spam, unrelated ads or proselytism 7. No post naming another member in order to criticize her or him 8. No post on current politics and leaders, too divisive and controversial 9. Do not block an admin, you will be banned from the group 10. Keep comments positive with politeness and civility 11. Because they usually trigger controversy, posts directly or indirectly on Jordan Peterson should be on our sister group. https://www.facebook.com/groups/1412635142104041/ ***Description of this group*** A liberal, open forum concerning C.G. Jung, myth, the Inner Task, Creative work. Art, writing, poetry, music, dance, dreams, anything that is numinous. A sacred space for discussing the psyche and its role in healing, wholeness and creative growth. Most welcome and encouraged are any posts promoting books, events, etc. Use the event calendar or post links to your book, or related business. No admins will be editing anything remotely relevant and civil. This group is an open template to express, explore and share your intuition, unconscious, or any information you think is important. The premise is not to have anyone interfere with your expression and to have a group "democracy of the heart." Please be "your own" admin. Encourage sharing, civility, and discussion with kindness and consideration. Disengage and walk away from threads if necessary. Do not ruin your day by interchanges on Facebook. Please block any member who annoys you or who you may have "typological" problems with. In the upper right of their post, there is an x. If you hover over it you will see "hide". Click on that and below to the left there is an option to block the person. The group admins are acting primarily as caretakers of YOUR group, not as leaders or guides, except perhaps by their personality showing through their posts. They will deal with the hopefully rare existential threats humanely but reluctantly according to the basic guidelines which are only common sense. Remember, everyone here is in reality and actually a Thou with a soul, not an It. We all have parents, children and people we love and deep, rich life experience. Please do not disrupt the free flow of sharing or sense of a safe place by discourtesy. Be kind whenever possible, as the Dalai Lama says, "and it's always possible" with restraint in tongue and pen. We are all at different points on the same path. Give hints to beginners, learn and be inspired by others. Namaste... (My soul bows to yours and I love you.)

Bullying of any kind isn't allowed, and degrading comments about things like race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. Avoid posts which may affect sentiments of any other individual or community. 3. Respect Everyone's Privacy Being part of this group requires mutual trust. No unsolicited messages or derogatory / abusive language will be tolerated. Members flouting any rules may or/and will be blocked without any notice. 4. Allowed Post Content Posts that help the community of this group are welcome. Posts should be related to group title/topic/category and in English language only. Posts in other languages will be declined. 5 Max 5 pictures per post will be allowed. Posts should not have links to any other websites or other Facebook page(s) or group(s). You can add a WhatsApp link or phone number. 6. General vs Promotional / Advertisement post days Promotional / Advertisement will be allowed free of cost only on Tuesdays and Fridays. On other days only paid advertisements will be allowed. For Pricing/customised package, get in touch with Admins. 7. For Facebook Marketers / Sale posts Either mention the price correctly or inbox the price when requested. Those not responding to price requests will not be allowed further posts. 8. DISCLAIMER – Group Admin not responsible for deals Please be sure of all deal aspects before entering in any deal and save yourself from any fraud, cheating, failed financial transaction, Non-delivery, deficiency in product or service, things sold. 9. DISCLAIMER – Buyer/Seller responsible for deals All buy/sell transactions are between members (buyer and the seller) only. Only both buyers and sellers are responsible for financial transactions. You can report members to Facebook. 10. Reporting All the members have the option and should exercise the option to REPORT any objectionable content / post / stalker / member flouting group rules.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Tree identification
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Goals and purpose - To provide a forum for tree identification and discussion specifically about identification characteristics. For this page, we consider any woody plant to fall within our purpose. Guidelines Location: - Maybe the most important clue for helping us determine an ID. What part of the world? e.g. country, state, province, city, etc. This is critical to help us and we insist on it. Your post may be removed without adding a location. - If posting a tree for identification, include as many details as you can. If commenting, approach with a collaborative mentality. Post as many ID requests as you like but please post one species at a time. . Pictures: Make note with your original post if your posting is an ID request of an unknown tree or posting an educational quiz, please limit these type quizzes to no more than 2 a day and periods of inactivity. Educational posts on identification characteristics are welcome, but please limit those also. Take clear pictures of features such as leaves, flowers, fruit, twigs including buds and leaf scars, bark, growth form. To help your camera focus on twigs etc., you can place your hand behind the item of interest. Habitat: Does the tree appear to have been intentionally planted, or is it growing wild? Is the tree in or near a city/town/village, or more of a remote location? General location (e.g. hilltop, lakeshore, riverbank, south-facing slope, etc.). Do: Read previous comments before commenting. "Like" IDs that you agree with. Repeat and redundant ID comments only bump up an already identified tree and could push unidentified plants further down. We WILL on occasion remove repeat ID's. If you are a repeat offender, you may be removed from the page. Add a comment if you have something new to say. If you disagree with a winning-by-voting ID, give reasons why. We are trying to focus on Trees so we also ask that you not post ID requests for anything that is not a tree or woody plant. . Don't - Things that will get you removed and/or banned from the page: blocking an admin or moderator, uncivil behavior or ad hominem attacks on another member, personal promotion of a business or product, or bringing politics into the forum. We have members with varying degrees of experience and knowledge so please keep that in mind and show respect. If you have issue with any post, please report to administrators or moderators or contact them by private message. Starting a complaint post and calling out an admin or moderator on a separate post will probably get you banned. Send a PM. We do not do classroom assignments. We reserve the right to remove at our discretion. Have fun and enjoy. For non woody plants, you may want to try the Plant Identification group or for discussion the Plant ID and discussion group. Plant Identification https://www.facebook.com/groups/156706504394635/ Plant Identification and discussion https://www.facebook.com/groups/623997204362467/ 
                </div>
               </div>

                 "Dear members of our Group – 'Archaeology, History and Art' As the group name indicates, our members are International and they are looking forward to enjoy an educative world History and Archaeology related digital experience in this group. You are all welcome to share interesting posts. However, there are rules. The rules are few in number and strongly recommended. 1. The group has zero tolerance for any offensive or/and abusive language or posts addressing any one of our members in person. 2. No racial, religious or political abusive or/and discriminatory language or photos. 3. Please limit postings to 3 posts per 24-hour period, so as not to overwhelm the timeline. 4. No sharing of other Facebook groups. We have created this group to be completely different from the other groups on FB and we would like to keep it that way. We here appreciate and encourage originality, credibility and taking initiative in creating your own posts, as an active involvement in the group activities. We don’t want this group transforms into something- which most of the FB groups eventually became - featureless automatically reposting from the same public groups over and over again. 5. Our group is an English Language group so to keep it accessible comments will need to be in English. Original posts in English with an accompanying translation from another language will be accepted though. 6. Members are expected to demonstrate self respect and respect for all other members with different views, after all we are in a Group because we share a passion for Archaeology, History and Art, let us all enjoy it. "

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Immortality
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is dedicated towards raising awareness about emerging technologies that have the potential to contribute positively to the human lifespan. We are finally approaching a point where we can more effectively negotiate our terms with death. ...we are on the verge of transcending our biological constraints and finally defeating death. [Further explanation] Throughout human history our species has attempted to grapple with death by trying to understand it, by trying to predict it, and by trying to defeat it... Over the last fifteen thousand years, the communities humanity has built upon the Earth have changed dramatically. We have moved from being a hunter &amp; gatherer-based species, to essentially maintaining globalized civilization capable of sending machines millions of kilometers deep into space to chunks of rock virgin to the hands of humanity... As our species first began to develop and refine language and began to construct relatively large communities, they also tried to explain and rationalize why death occurs, and how they might be able to prevent it... However, as our ancient fore-bearers lacked deep naturalistic understanding of their environment, little progress was made toward dealing with death. Gods and rituals were used to place a handle on death, it provided simplistic explanations and methods for displaying grief and respect... but this was still inadequate. Over the past 300 years, as our species finally harnessed the power of electricity, and started on its path toward understanding its own construction, we have made great leaps in our understanding of our environment, and ourselves. We have reached a stage in our development where it is beginning to look as if we may be able to slow or even prevent the damaging effects of aging at a cellular level, and it seems that we are rapidly approaching a point where we will finally break free from our biological constraints. The word "Immortality" has always had a connotation of mysticism and magic attached to it, and since there has so far been no alternative to death, it has been seen as a fantasy to distract us from its inevitability... but we must realize that with each scientific discovery, it provides a stepping stone towards the next, and that combined with our powers of abstract reasoning, our innate curiosity, and our relentless determination, we can dismount this word from the web of fiction it is currently entangled in, and bring it into the scientific realm. In short, we are on the verge of a transformation, our scientific understanding of the mechanics of the universe has been increasing exponentially... in the coming decades as the fields of Bioengineering, Genetics, Nano-scale Technology, and Computing mature, we will begin to see a change in the meaning of life and death. We now have the ability to construct artificial hearts, we have utterly decimated entire viral species with our vaccines, we can control mechanical appendages with our minds, and cloning technology is maturing to the point where personalized organs can be and will be cloned when needed (which essentially means the end of death via organ failure... at least mostly)... so, as we progress we must maintain a strong sense of caution, but above all, we must remain open to the possibility of transcending our biological longevity limits... Possibly living as long as you wish. We can already see the tell-tale signs of this happening, and given an semi-optimistic estimate... we can expect to see some pretty amazing changes to the human life-span within the next 25 years, and if you try your best to take care of your body in concert with these emerging technologies, you can expect to live well past 2100 A.D. 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Society of Women Engineers - SWE Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This Facebook group exists for SWE members from all over the world to engage with each other and connect about issues and content relating to SWE and women engineers in general. As with all SWE activities, this group will reflect the core values of SWE which are posted below. Any posts and discussions not upholding these values will be removed. Please do not post commercial messages or job postings on this page. Use the community to share successes, challenges, constructive feedback, questions and goals. Contact people directly with product and service information if you believe it would help them. SWE has a robust job posting site: https://careers.swe.org/ to promote corporate openings. SWE Core Values: Integrity: We aspire to the highest level of ethical behavior as evidenced by honesty and dignity in our personal and professional relationships and responsibilities. Inclusive Environment: We embrace diversity in its broadest interpretation and commit to creating an inclusive environment for all our members and stakeholders. We value the contributions of a diverse membership, which enables SWE to achieve its full potential. Mutual Support: We provide an organization that fosters mentoring, and the development of professional and personal networks. Professional Excellence: We conduct our activities in a professional manner, demonstrating and demanding the highest standards of business practices. Trust: We share a common definition of success with open, transparent access to common information, building mutual respect and confidence in the competence of those with whom we lead, serve and partner with.
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Anthropology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 “Diverse viewpoints are important for generating novel ideas that eventually are sifted out to yield the most comprehensive, logical, coherent, and empirically verifiable one at a particular time.” The actual essence of the group is cumulative-reciprocal learning ensuring mutual respect. For us, the purpose of Anthropology is to generate knowledge and stimulate anthropological thoughts. We are here to discuss different issues; share personal thoughts, experiences, and ideas. As Malcolm Forbes quoted "Diversity: the art of thinking independently together". No comment/quires are “stupid/non-logical/irrelevant (although there are few)”. We are learning every day, through a dialogue-based learning approach. Members of this group represent students-academic-researchers with diverse academic backgrounds. And we believe, along with anthropological approaches, multidisciplinary or trans-disciplinary approaches will enrich anthropology. We do welcome diverse thoughts and accept multiple realities. Given that we are a very large family now, we will follow some basic principles: While posting: 1. Please provide a brief (even though it is very brief) description of the post, in English. 2. Please write something about the link or picture that you're posting. Express as little as five lines on the post, so as to make the discussion more valuable. 3. Please report us about offensive comments and posts those do not have any anthropological relevance. And of course, report us about random links of pornography, products and personal pages. While making a comment on a post: 1. Do ask questions, make comments and constructive criticisms, do not make personal attacks. 2. Please consider that we all know the difference between “freedom of speech” and “making extraneous and off-topic” comments. 3. We may have distinctive cultural outlook to understand only the culturally relative phenomenon of his/her niche. Please do not be too judgmental. We will remove: 1. Links or pictures without a brief description or the member's views about it. 2. Questions that look like exam or assignment questions. 3. Offensive posts and comments directed towards another member, admins or the creator of the group. 4. Any ethnocentric or prejudiced comment that is based on a member's race, ethnicity, nationality, class, caste, religion, belief, sex, language, sexual orientation, gender identity, age, health or other status. In extreme cases, we might delete the member who does not fulfill these principles. This group was created on April 20, 2008.
                </div>
               </div>

God Bless you in your endeavors! #1 RULE- Treat others as you would like to be treated ! If I find out you are not, I will not hesitate to remove and block you. #2 Rule- ALL TRANSACTIONS ARE BETWEEN BUYER &amp; SELLER and at your own risk. Admins are not here to handle disputes. TIPS TO HELP~ USE PAYPAL it offers protection, NEVER use anything but the GOODS &amp; Services option or you lose proctection. PAYPAL fees are part of doing business, do NOT charge your buyer your Paypal fees, simply figure that into the cost along with your packing if desired. PACK WELL, make sure your items are secure and can not shift during shipping. If you have a high priced order insist on using insurance at the Post Office. I love my fellow homeschool Mamas and hope I can continue to serve you.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Home Theater Enthusiasts is a group for anyone who loves and enjoys home theater, wants to learn more about it, and wants to take their own home theater to the next level. Here's what we want at HTE: We want elevated conversation. We want fun and friendly, but mature and respectful. We want quality posting. We want information shared that helps us all achieve the best possible experience in our home theaters. Here's what we don't want at HTE: Bickering. Extreme "fanboyism". Unhelpful posts that just clog the page. Disrespectful comments or personal attacks. Useless off-topic posts. Advertising or self-promotion. Posts about torrents, cams, or plugins to enable illicit content sharing; we don't condone copyright theft and we won't support it. We also kindly ask that you don't make numerous posts that aren't constructive or helpful. When you post, consider that thousands of people will see your post in their feed. Is it something they'll appreciate, or just something they'll have to scroll past? Making a post about your new projector, another post of it coming out of the box, another when you mount it, another with screenshots. Here are a few questions to ask yourself before you post: 1. Can something be learned from this? Will this help somebody else? 2. Have I searched to see if the question I’m asking has been asked before? Can it produce answers that aren’t completely subjective? Will it create an interesting and effective discussion? 3. Did I write this in way that makes me sound like an intelligent person? Read it. Can people understand your intent? 4. Am I asserting that the way I do something is the only way, or am I simply telling them how I do it? 5. Am I answering questions based on sound science combined with experience and knowledge, or am I just regurgitating something I read somewhere? 6. If I am posting an opinion, am I contradicting someone with far more experience than my own? 7. Would I want this on my page if I were a moderator of a group? Think before you post, and enjoy HTE!
                </div>
               </div>

                 Society for the Teaching of Psychology - STP
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Society for the Teaching of Psychology promotes excellence in the teaching and learning of psychology. The Society provides resources and services, access to a global collaborative community, and opportunities for professional development. The Society also strives to advance the scholarship of teaching and learning, advocate for the needs of teachers of psychology, foster partnerships across academic settings, and increase recognition of the value of the teaching profession. This is a public group where STP members and others interested in high school and university teaching of psychology can discuss pedagogy and professional development. The Society for the Teaching of Psychology (STP) is Division 2 of the American Psychological Association. Renew your membership or join here: http://teachpsych.org/join

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for elementary teachers and users of Math in Practice, a K-5 teacher support resource from Sue O'Connell and colleagues, published by Heinemann. Ask questions about teaching math, share challenges and strategies, and talk about how you use Math in Practice in your classroom each day. Learn more about Math in Practice at http://MathInPractice.com Math in Practice is a comprehensive, grade-by-grade professional learning resource designed to fit with any math program or curriculum you are using. Created with elementary teachers in mind, Math in Practice focuses on developing deep content knowledge, exploring effective instructional strategies, and providing extensive tasks, activities, and teacher notes. Each grade-level book includes a wealth of corresponding online resources that provide classroom-ready tools for enhancing instruction.
