                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome everyone! The purpose of this group is to promote discussions and dissemination of cognitive behavioral therapy (CBT) knowledge! You can also use this forum to promote your books, workshops, apps, conferences, etc. - as long as they are related to CBT! There are just a few simple rules: (1) Stay on topic (CBT)! (2) Mental health professionals in this group should never post confidential patient information! (3) This is not a support group, so members should not post questions seeking advice on personal issues! (4) If you try to post spam you will be removed from the group! (5) Be kind and supportive to one another! If you see a post you think is disrespectful, please report it! Thanks, Dr. Simon Rego

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 High School Mathematics
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 If you need a little help in high school mathematics or have some time to help someone in high school mathematics, you are more than welcome to join this group aptly named 'High School Mathematics' and has the web address https://www.facebook.com/groups/highschool.mathematics/ Here are some guidelines for the group: 1. Topics may include Algebra, Statistics, Probability, Coordinate Geometry, Precalculus, Differential &amp; Integral Calculus, Multivariable Calculus, Linear Algebra (Matrix Theory) and Differential Equations. 2. Use only English to post and comment. 3. Post only math questions of appropriate level in which you are having difficulty or need some explanation. 4. Be polite and respectful to other members. 5. Post detail solutions only unless asked to provide just the answer. 6. Do not post any kind of advertisement or link to any websites in any post or comment. 7. Do not share any post from any timeline in Facebook, be that from your own timeline, or a Facebook page or Facebook group's timeline. 8. Do not comment with an answer if that answer has already been provided. You may click like to the already provided correct answer. In fact, you are encouraged to do so. If you have an alternate method for an answer, by all means please feel free to provide in the comments. 9. Do not post a question that has been posted recently. 10. Do not flood the group with several questions at the same time. 11. Try not to post questions by taking a picture from the textbook. Type it out as best as you can. Avoid misunderstanding by appropriate use of parentheses. 12. If you must post an image because it is a Geometry problem, it better be your own image, not something you picked up in the web, and add your own description of the problem. 13. Do not ask fellow members to add you as friend, do not engage in exchanging personal information in the comments. Give other members their privacy. 14. Do not try to post thanking any of the admins for accepting you to the group. 15. Always listen to the admins.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ancient Origins Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the www.Ancient-Origins.net Facebook Group At Ancient Origins we believe that one of the most important fields of knowledge we can pursue as human beings is our beginnings. With this in mind, our goal is to highlight the very latest archaeological findings, peer-reviewed academic research and evidence, as well as offering alternative viewpoints and explanations of science, archaeology, mythology, religion and history around the globe. We’re the only Pop Archaeology site combining scientific research with out-of-the-box perspectives. By bringing together top experts and authors, we explore lost civilizations, examine sacred writings, tour ancient places, and question mysterious happenings. Our open community is dedicated to digging into the origins of our species on planet earth, and question wherever the discoveries might take us. We seek to retell the story of our beginnings. RULES OF POSTING We strive to ensure that Ancient Origins is a constructive, non-discriminatory, and friendly place to discuss a wide variety of topics. To maintain a positive atmosphere and to promote constructive discussion, we ask that you adhere to these simple guidelines. • Respect - Our aim is to make each of our members feel welcome. Racism, religious intolerance, and any kind of discrimination have no place in our group. • Be polite – You are free to disagree, share opposing views, and debate a topic, but please be civil. We will not tolerate posts which insult, belittle, bait or otherwise antagonise group members. • Quality – We want our group to be packed full of quality material, fascinating stories, and interesting discussions. Postings that are vulgar, profane, crude, sexist, racist, homophobic, pornographic, or defamatory, are not considered ‘quality’ material and will be removed. • Promote others not yourselves – you are welcome to recommend great books, websites or quality material you have come across relating to ancient origins. But our group is not the place for advertising and self-promotion. The group moderators shall have full discretion to address any behaviour that they feel is inappropriate, such as by warning, deleting comments or banning. The bottom line is that we want Ancient Origins to be an enjoyable and constructive environment for everyone.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Elite Math Circle
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is formed for all those individuals who have the passion and interest in learning and improving their mathematical abilities. This group aims to serve as channel for exchange of brilliant ideas regarding the wonderful world of mathematics. Math wizards, Mathematicians, Mathemagicians, Math Majors, Math Enthusiasts, Math Fanatics, Math Quizzers, Math Professors and Teachers, Math Students and even Math Haters are very much welcome in this group. It is highly recommended that you may post any worthwhile discussion topics, particularly about math. Enjoy viewing our group! Hope that everyone be benefited in this group!!! ************************************************************************************************************************************************************ Due to the growing EMC, us admins felt the need to set in stone 10 rules to remember when posting in the group. This will be in effect starting today, 17Aug2014. Please be guided accordingly, thank you. ================================== EMC Ten Commandments . 1. Use English at all times. - Contrary to popular belief, this is not an all-pinoy group. . 2. Do not be a grammar nazi. - This is a math group, not a grammar group. . 3. Do not trashtalk. - Taunts count as well. Avoid kindling flames at all cost. . 4. Do not post topics unrelated to math. - Please use your own walls for these. . 5. Do not be lazy. - Google is there if you don't know how to get started with your homework. Don't post in EMC raising the white flag without even trying to solve. . 6. Do not cheat. - Posting exam questions before or during exam proper is not allowed. . 7. Do not spam. - If you can't see your post, do not repost. Most probably it was removed due to a violation of the rules. . 8. Check the "Terms of Use" of your source. - Sites like Brilliant.org disallow the public display of their materials. . 9. Be clear about problems you post. - Ambiguous problems like 25/5*2 are not allowed. These are made without the intent to be solved, otherwise the necessary amount of parentheses would have been provided. . 10. Do not spoonfeed. - Please use hints only when asked for help. Posting the complete solution does not help the other person-- it's actually yourself you are helping (to feel good, maybe). Let us live by the proverb: "Give a man a fish and you feed him for a day; teach a man to fish and you feed him for a lifetime". Have a nice day and enjoy! . --EMC Admins-- . . ================================== EMC Elite Members (these are non admin members who have shown great skills in Math, in random order. They are more likely to be promoted as EMC Admin) . Ryan Caduyac . Dever Magtibay . Reyman Jan Evangelista . Kristian Villamayor . Kennard Sychingping . John Lester Tan . Christian Baldo . (List will be updated time to time...)

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Archaeology News Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Archaeology News Network is an online open access, pro-community news site bringing together people in related fields with active interests intersecting archaeology. It may be found here: http://archaeologynewsnetwork.blogspot.com/ Because we have been experiencing problems with posting on this facebook group we are now choosing to provide members with some TANN guidelines, well actually they are more like rules, break them and you will be removed, These are: No commercial activities: no false accounts carrying malware pretending to be advertisements for shoes, sunglasses, or computer gadgets will be tolerated here, also general commercial activities will get you removed from the group without discussion. No looted archaeological objects: The illegal excavation and sale of antiquities is completely unacceptable on this page (and beyond). This group will act immediately to remove posters advocating this or attempting to trade in antiquities. Stay on topic: this group is called ‘The Archaeological News Network’. Any posts involving ufos, aliens, new age pseudo science or mysticism, religion, politics or nationalistic content will not be permitted. This is a page dedicated to sharing up to date and verifiable research and not for personal agendas or private conjecture. In addition this is not a page for posting innumerable pretty pictures of objects (or scenery), objects are only archaeology if they have a background, if you think an object or place has value, post it and cite properly its source and credit the photographer or museum collection. Breach of copyright of images is illegal. Equally, do not individually post whole albums of photographs. This pushes the news off the page: post a link to an album you think has value. Try to cite your sources when posting, and readers try to remember, this is the internet, always verify statements that are posted anywhere on fb, we the admins here do not have time to verify the veracity of every object or every post, so we depend on you all to think before assuming random posts are absolutely positively correct. Also we have many cultures and languages represented here in this group and they all have something to offer us and to learn from, basic good manners and cultural tolerance is required of you all. Members are encouraged to post news articles in their own languages. Cheers from the TANN admins

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ecopsychology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The basic idea of ecopsychology is that while the human mind is shaped by the modern social world, it can be readily inspired and comforted by the wider natural world, because that is the arena in which it originally evolved. Mental health or unhealth cannot be understood simply in the narrow context of only intrapsychic phenomena or social relations. One also has to include the relationship of humans to other species and ecosystems. These relations have a deep evolutionary history; reach a natural affinity within the structure of their brains and they have deep psychic significance in the present time, in spite of urbanization. Humans are dependent on healthy nature not only for their physical sustenance, but for mental health, too. The destruction of ecosystems means that something in humans also dies. http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecopsychology
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Historical Archaeology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 For the purposes of this group, and as it is defined in the profession, historical archaeology focuses on the post-medieval world and, for many, the spread of capitalism. Please note, this is meant to be a group for professionals and student archaeologists or historians. It is not meant to promote "privy digging" or grave robbing, or to be a place to discuss the "archaeologies" of Atlantis, etc. This is a collegial gathering. We do not always share the same opinions, but we do share an interest in historical archaeology. If you are unable to interact with others in a respectful way, or post inflammatory remarks, or leave posts that are unrelated to the topic, you will be removed from the group. Membership is gained only by answering ALL entry questions AND agreeing to the rules.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Counselling and Psychotherapy Jobs
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 What is this group (Anyone who wishes to see or contribute to Counselling and Psychotherapy jobs anywhere) Let’s be a community of people who endeavour to use this site for our own purposes and to share our employment knowledge to benefit all of us. As a counsellor and psychotherapist I want to encourage a group where anyone can advertise salaried therapy jobs worldwide and where therapy job seekers may express interest in salaried work. All salaried job postings are free! I don’t want this to be a political area however I feel strongly about student and also qualified therapist having to raise between 300 and 450 clinical hours prior to being paid. Whilst it is great to volunteer for charities and good causes, these clinical hours are restricting thousands of paid jobs. Current students are desperate to volunteer and therefore these jobs remain in the voluntary sector and not always by proper charities. This can prevent job progression and also leaving qualified therapist unemployed and the private market saturated. This in turn brings down the potential earning of us all. Whilst there is no actual answer, I thought it would be fruitful for us to share our information and make it easier for potential employers to reach us directly. Since starting the group at 5.00pm on 22 March 2018 the group has grown both nationally and internationally. I am often approached for advertising purposes. Should you wish speak to this audience outside of the free job posting rule, please contact me billi@billisilverstein.co.uk. You may advertise on my sister website Counselling and Psychotherapy jobs which promotes all postings on multi-media platforms including this Facebook page. Also on twitter @billistherapy This is not a space for personal promotion or to publicise your private practice/services but a chance for you to highlight yourself to prospective employers. Please also share any jobs you may know of within our sector. General Rules: Posts will be reviewed for approval. Please be mindful about your expressions and language. Inappropriate posts or comments will be removed wherever spotted. Members may be removed at any time. Members may not message other members trying to sell or promote themselves. Please respond to questions or queries on threads. Do not respond to other members privately without invitation. Respect for the group and its content is vital. Free posting rules 1. Please head up your job listing with which Country, City and Area the job is in. 2. Only post in English 3. No MLM, spammers or non-job advertisement 4. Anyone found spamming will be removed.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Microbiology
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Group For All Microbiologists and who are interested in Microbiology Science Please All of us share anything useful and related to Microbiology so we can get the benefits together ..... and please invite all ur microbiologists friends Microbiology (from Greek μῑκρος, mīkros, "small"; βίος, bios, "life"; and -λογία, -logia) is the study of microorganisms, which are unicellular or cell-cluster microscopic organisms. This includes eukaryote such as fungi and protists, and prokaryotes, which are bacteria and archaea. Viruses, though not strictly classed as living organisms, are also studied. In short; microbiology refers to the study of life and organisms that are too small to be seen with the naked eye. Microbiology is a broad term which includes virology, mycology, parasitology, bacteriology and other branches. A microbiologist is a specialist in microbiology. Microbiology is researched actively, and the field is advancing continually. We have probably only studied about one percent of all of the microbe species on Earth. Although microbes were first observed over three hundred years ago, the field of microbiology can be said to be in its infancy relative to older biological disciplines such as zoology and botany.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Divi Theme Users
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is the official Elegant Themes Divi Theme User Facebook group. It was founded by Divi users who love Divi and want to build up the Divi community. It remains community-based &amp; is community moderated by amazing volunteers &amp; fans of the Divi theme. Elegant Themes does its best to make sure the group stays focused on the community atmosphere that it started with. GENERAL POSTING RULES &amp; GUIDELINES First, please scroll down to the bottom of the About tab and review the rules in the official rule section. Below we've included some additional guidelines: Place *SOLVED* at the top of your posts after you get your questions answered successfully. This forum is not a job board of any kind. Please refrain from asking for partnerships, developers to DM for or asking people to contribute to your business paid or unpaid. If we receive reports of unsolicited PM messages asking for work, your profile will be deleted – if a user asks people to PM them for extra help – then that is cool, but do try to solve the issue in an open forum manner as this helps everyone. Do not offer paid help within threads. We will delete these comments as and when we see them. You will be warned and if it is a repeat offense then you will be suspended or banned. Please search the group prior to asking a question before asking what the BEST solution is. Good Citizenship is the motto here. Keep this group for Divi related subjects. With over 47,000 members and growing, we cannot keep up with the many other NDR issues. Please refer to another group directly related to non-Divi subjects. This group is for Divi users. If you aren't a user of Divi or if you are posting about something non-Divi related, you will likely be removed from the group. Hosting is an emotive subject, please refrain from asking for advice on which host to use. If you buy cheap, you get cheap. SPECIAL POSTING DAY GUIDELINES While every day is help day, we've created the following special sharing days. For each of these days, we will post a pinned mega thread. Themed sharing is ONLY allowed within that thread. Individual posts outside of our mega threads will be treated as spam. Moderator Monday - Learn all about your moderators &amp; how we moderate. Tutorial Tuesday - If you’ve created a Divi tutorial within the last week (dates must be visible on the post) then you are free to post a link to it in the Tutorial Tuesday mega thread. Web Design Wednesday - Show off your latest Divi designs in the Web Design Wednesday mega thread. These can be client or personal sites. Product Thursday - Have you created a Divi related product? Share it with the whole community by posting a link in the Product Thursday mega thread. Freebie Friday - If you've created a Divi freebie, this is the thread where you can share that with the whole group. Give a little and you will get A LOT. Thank you for being here :)

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Mushroom Identification Page
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ THIS. 1) 1 species per post, it makes the ID's made in the comments more accessible 2) Tell us where in the World you are? Location can be VERY important. 3) Take pictures of: - top of the cap - underside of the cap - stipe (preferably the whole stipe with the base) - if possible, a longitudinal section to see the context (flesh of the mushroom) and the attachement of the hymenium (gills, tubes, spines, etc) to the stipe' - overview/side view - as many different ages, from small buttons to worn out mushrooms - spore print 3) Make sure that these pictures are: - made preferably in situ (on location), but if that is not possible, then use a neutral background - in the right white balance (colours of the picture should resemble the real colours in daylight) - not too dark or over-exposed (preferably in daylight) - sharp - free of distracting elements like leafs, twigs, dirt etc. The specimen and characteristics have to be clearly visible 4) Always include the following in the description: 4a) if you already have an idea of what species it may be, add: - the name (both scientific and common) - a description of the characteristics you base your ID on - the sources you used for identification (books/websites) 4b) If you don't know what it is: - scent - taste (it is not harmful to nibble a bit off of a mushroom and chew on it for 10 sec. BUT ALWAYS SPIT IT OUT! Even if it tastes nice! Amanita phalloides has quite a slight sweet flavour, but you don't want to swallow a piece of that...) - the true colours (if the colours in the picture does not resemble the true colours by daylight) - possible discolouration of the cap/stipe/hymenium/context (this may take a while with some species) - the substrate (mulch/wood/living tree/bare ground/dead animals etc) - habitat (nearest tree species, woods, calcareous grassland, fen, dry/moist soil, high/low elevation etc) - location (if in US: state/region; if abroad: country + region) 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">17&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">222 篇新帖</span></span>

                 Plexaholics
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 See below for Rules / Reglas del grupo This is a group for all things Plex. Sharing, Help and fun. Rules: NO LEECHING Do not join and just start asking for shares. We are here to help, and will gladly assist you in setting up your own server unless someone has said they are looking for users. Offering to share in return for shares is allowed. NO SELLING We do not allow any solicitation of sales or "trials" to Plex or IPTV services. Any selling beyond (personal equipment, new apps) that please check with a Mod or Admin. DON'T BE RUDE We are here to help and have fun and talk Plex and other tech topics. You are allowed to speak your mind here...but when it turns to attacking and name calling another member that is not allowed. Depending on the offense we will do one of the following: Mute you from commenting for a certain amount of time. Boot you from the group....you can rejoin if you wish after cooling down. Ban you from the group and not allow you back. We will try and warn you before doing this....but if you are out of control, then we will just do one of the above. TOPICS It doesn't have to be Plex related! If it's about a NAS, or new ISP, or discounts on hardware, or a question about some weird software feature in some related app...it's OK. On the other hand, if the only conversation your post will create is one that is the opposite of the above - then it will be removed, and depending on the topic - subject to immediate removal or banishment. Politiks, religion, racism, and other bigoted topics may be cause for immediate removal from the group. In short - we're here to have fun and be a community. If it's not going to contribute to that idea...don't post it. DON'T PM PEOPLE AND ASK TO BE ADDED. There are plenty of people who will post that they are sharing. They might openly share or ask for a "Share 4 Share'. Keep the requests in the group. IF A POST IS DELETED If your post gets deleted the mods will do our best to PM you why it was removed. So, check you PM's if your post goes missing. *** IF RULES ARE NOT FOLLOWED YOU WILL BE REMOVED*** Reglas del grupo: NO SER PEDINCHES No se unan al grupo y comienzen a pedir que los agreguen a plex. Estamos aqui para ayudarlos y gustosamente les ayudaremos a montar su propio servidor. PROHIBIDAS LAS VENTAS No se permite ninguna conversacion/post referente a ventas del servicio plex o canales de tv. NO INSULTAR Estamos aqui para ayudar,intercambiar ideas,hablar de plex y divertirnos. NO MANDAR MENSAJES PRIVADOS PIDIENDO SER AGREGADO AL SERVIDOR Siempre habra varios usuarios dispuestos a compartir su servidor,podria ser compartir sin nada a cambio o compartir a cambio de que tambien le compartan ustedes. ***SI NO SIGUES LAS REGLAS SERAS REMOVIDO DEL GRUPO***

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ancestral Plants
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is designed to help stand in for the lack of plant-knowledgeable elders in our societies. People here can share knowledge and ask questions about the diversity of plants and how people can interact with them in a conscientious manner. Here are the "rules" (which are really just guidelines): 1. You can post information and ask questions about any content regarding plants, but this group is primarily for the discovery of wild plants and how they can benefit humans and landscapes. Therefore, identification and use questions are acceptable. Further, discussions are not limited to politically correct topics. Suggested topics include: plant taxonomy and identification edible plants medicinal plants entheogenic plants utilitarian plants indigenous use of plants conscientious harvesting methods beauty and artistic appreciation (This group is not the ideal location for cultivated plants, food crops, and the like, but such questions will not be discouraged.) 2. If you post information about a plant, it should be based on reports of historical observations, modern study, and/or personal experience. If you cannot support your statements in this way, please note that you are posting an opinion. 3. Be courteous. If you are here to support your pathologically adolescent ego, please find another group. This is a place to support and bolster people's excitement about plants. Sometimes we may disagree (and that is ok--it can be done politely). 4. Advertisements aren't to be excluded (for plant learning), but you should seek approval by an admin to confirm it fits in with the theme of Ancestral Plants. 5. Show gratitude for the people that take time to provide you with information. This is a good way to keep quality admins on the site (so that they feel their efforts are valued). 6. This is not a place to project your fears onto other people. If you are afraid of interacting with wild plants, please keep your opinions to yourself or express your concerns from a place of respect and open-mindedness. The fact is, this industrial society has conditioned you to be afraid of the wild and your fears are almost certainly exaggerated. Likewise, if you feel every health ailment needs to be examined by a health specialist that has been trained in and credentialed by Industrial Medicine (i.e., Western Medicine), this may not be the best group for you. While Industrial Medicine has its strengths, it also has weaknesses. This is a place for helping people build sovereignty, something that can't happen when everyone is deeply steeped in "appeal to authority". Suggesting someone see a doctor is different from attacking someone for looking for alternative opinions. The latter won't be accepted. Let's make Ancestral Plants an approachable, exciting, and useful group. We can only do that with cooperation and the understanding that we can't survive without plants--so lets not do anything to dissuade anyone from learning about wild plants. 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 U.S. Army Combat Engineers and Sappers Worldwide
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for any and all who have served as a Combat Engineer worldwide. This is not a place to advertise or sell things. It is so that we can all get together and stay connected where ever we might be now. A sapper, also called pioneer or combat engineer, is a combatant or soldier who performs a variety of military engineering duties such as bridge-building, laying or clearing minefields, demolitions, field defences and general construction, as well as road and airfield construction and repair. They are also trained to serve as infantry personnel in defensive and offensive operations. A sapper's duties are devoted to tasks involving facilitating movement of allied forces and impeding those of enemies . The term "sapper" is used in the British Army, Polish Army, Commonwealth nations and the U.S. military. The phrase "sapper" come from the French word "sap" which means to dig or to trench. Sappers lead the way!

This is a FREE group that I run and I don’t have the time to contemplate how to manage each post/comment, so if you don’t follow the rules you will be removed and banned from the group. I have built this community to support and educate. I want to make sure it’s a safe space and that I preserve the quality of the group at all times, which is why I have developed these rules and enforce them on a daily basis.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Prehistoric Society facebook group! This is the place to find lots of info about anything pertaining to human prehistory from the earliest human origins, through to the emergence of written records. We have very few rules, but the few we have are important: 1) play nice 2) include a little information about your post rather than just linking to websites 3) do not spam ...and last, but certainly not least, 4) no dinosaurs please as we ain't that kind of prehistory! And if you like what you see here, please think about joining the Society at www.prehistoricsociety.org/join . Annual membership includes the journal PPS and free online access to all journals back to 1905, three newsletters, many events, postage and much more... and all for £35 for individuals, £17.50 for students and £25 for retired people. Well worth it! 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Viddyoze Users
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! New here? Please watch this video: www.viddyoze.com/welcome/ Now, the boring bits... This group is not a support channel for issues. IF you have any issues or queries re products, please email support@viddyoze.com What you can do in this group: 1 - Share your content for positive and constructive feedback 2 - Share ideas and concepts that promote the positive and creative development of video content 3 - Compose posts asking questions to the group on 'how to's' 'ideas for' etc. What you cannot do in this group: The following will not be tolerated: Sexist, racist, homophobic, transphobic, ableist, etc. content is subject to moderation. Off topic posts, worthless posts, bumping, etc, will be moderated and removed. Repeat posting of the same off topic posts and spamming of links that have nothing to do with the subject at hand will be banned outright. Political or Religious views Trolling will be squashed whenever possible/reported/found out. Posting people's personal information on the page is prohibited. If you want to question a ban, also email abuse, we're open to discussion. Freedom of speech does not include freedom to be abusive with language. Immediate deletion: Pornographic, or explicitly violent content not related to the Occupy movement. Any sort of hate speech against any group of people. Obvious spamming or flooding of the main page or group page. Inciting violence. Political campaign advertisements. Commercial advertisements. Blocking Admin or creating hollow facebook profiles. (If you have a second profile in order to be anonymous, please contact Admin and we will reconsider certain profiles. . . . We respect your rights of privacy.) personal attacks- keep on the topic of the thread and off the topic of an individual. Spamming Admin will result in Admin Block. User warnings and the banning: 1) User will be given one chance to self edit. If this is not done, 2) Admin will delete comment and may delete user. 3) User may contact Admin for re-admission into group, repeated offenses may result in 4) permanent deletion from group Procedures: Complaints and questions can be sent to Admin. Be sure to include a screen shot of offensive matter and a general idea of where it can be found. If a complaint is of a personal nature and you feel uncomfortable, you are always welcome to contact any admin directly. The admins will always respect free speech, given the above limits. The admins will keep records on warnings and banning. This is an evolving set of guidelines, subject to amendments.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Jungian Psychology &amp; Alchemy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for people interested in Carl Jung's concepts, theories and the concepts of hermetic alchemy that he revived. Anything off-topic will be deleted. If anybody posts multiple off-topic posts, they will be immediately removed from the group. Thanks! Any links promoting offsite venues for goods and services or donations will also be deleted. Types of links that can be posted: - Links to articles, videos and resources - Links to related forums or groups - Links to other Facebook pages - Links to other websites related to Jung, his theories and practices, analytical psychology, and Alchemy All links must be purely informational in nature, and not obviously made in order to sell any goods or services, or collect donations. Thanks for observing these simple guidelines! In terms of conversation, feel free to get personal, curious, theoretical and practical in discussions with others. Maybe some magic will come of this. Thanks for stopping by!

                 We are bunch of like-minded DIYers chatting about alternative uses for 18650 batteries! We highly recommend watching this video regarding diypowerwall safety https://youtu.be/tpfc-y3e0Gs RULES (Last Updated Feb 3rd, 2020) * English Only. Posts in a language other than English will be deleted without notice. Please use an online translator, if needed, when posting. * NO short links of any kind that obfuscate the destination website. * NO affiliate links of any kind. * NO GIFs or otherwise pointless memes. * NO commercial advertising; however, if you're an active contributing member (50+ posts) on the forum, feel free to list your advertisement ON the forum then link to your forum post in this group. DISCLAIMERS (Last Updated Feb 3rd, 2020) * Lithium batteries can be very dangerous, even when used in accordance with the manufacturer's instruction, and can result in fire, property damage, personal injury, and/or death. Information exchanged through this group should NOT be taken as "advice" or "how-to". You agree to accept full responsibility for your own actions and cannot hold any individual(s) liable for any resulting damages or injury. * All work should be done by a fully licensed and certified professional. This includes, but is not limited to, electrical installations, cabling, and construction. * Some of the links shared here to sites including, but not limited to, eBay, Amazon, and AliExpress, may contain affiliate tracking parameters. The person sharing the link may earn a small commission when a purchase is made. ADDITIONAL RESOURCES (Last Updated Feb 3rd, 2020) * Second Life Storage Forum &gt; https://secondlifestorage.com/ * Global Cell Counter &gt; https://secondlifestorage.com/cellcount.php * 18650 Cell Identification Database &gt; https://secondlifestorage.com/celldatabase.php * Repackr Pack Builder &gt; https://secondlifestorage.com/repacker.php

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is a place where anything related to plants trees and mushrooms can be discussed with the exception of medicinal and active/hallucinogenic mushrooms and plants. Read the post pinned at the top of the group for more detail description. - Group Guidelines - -Please read previous comments before helping ID and avoid guessing. -Please include your location when making ID requests, as we have group members from all over the world. -Avoid posting images of dead animals without content warnings. -No advertising or selling. -Personal insults, belittling, excessive shaming, or making fun of people will not be tolerated, members who feel the need to personally insult other members will be removed without notice. -Posts that are obviously spam, contain unsubstantiated health claims, graphic photos not hidden in comments, or that are completely off topic will be removed as well. -DO NOT JOKE about eating something especially if something is poisonous or suggest that people take potentially fatal risks. -This is not a group for the general or specific discussion of the production or consumption of hallucinogens. There are many other forums for this. - DO NOT BLOCK GROUP MODS OR ADMINS! Doing so will result in being removed from the group If you see something that does not belong please "report to admin" this works for both posts and individual comments. It requires a group effort to keep this community friendly, helpful and supportive. Thanks and enjoy

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Chemical Engineering
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Chemical engineering is the branch of engineering that deals with the application of physical science (e.g., chemistry and physics), and life sciences (e.g., biology, microbiology and biochemistry) with mathematics, to the process of converting raw materials or chemicals into more useful or valuable forms. In addition to producing useful materials, modern chemical engineering is also concerned with pioneering valuable new materials and techniques - such as nanotechnology, fuel cells and biomedical engineering. Chemical engineering largely involves the design, improvement and maintenance of processes involving chemical or biological transformations for large-scale manufacture. Chemical engineers ensure the processes are operated safely, sustainably and economically. Chemical engineers in this branch are usually employed under the title of process engineer. A related term with a wider definition is chemical technology. A person employed in this field is called a chemical engineer
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">14&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">3 篇新帖</span></span>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Geneticists - Biotechnologist - Molecular genetics
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A geneticist is a scientist who studies genetics, the science of heredity and variation of organisms. A geneticist can also be employed as a teacher or researcher. Some geneticists perform experiments and analyze data to interpret the inheritance of traits. Most geneticists complete at least a Bachelor’s degree and many continue on to a more advanced degree. Geneticists participate in courses from many areas, such as biology, chemistry, physics, microbiology, cell biology, English, and mathematics. They also participate in more specific genetics courses such as molecular genetics, transmission genetics, population genetics, quantitative genetics, ecological genetics, and genomics. Geneticists can work in many different fields, doing a variety of jobs. There are many careers for geneticists in medicine, agriculture, wildlife, general sciences or many other fields. Listed below are a few examples of careers a geneticist may pursue. Genetic counseling Gene therapy Pharmacogenomics Plant breeding Animal breeding Genomics Biotechnology Proteomics Microbial genetics Teaching Management of a Lab Sales and Marketing of science products Publishing of scientific material Patenting procedures Paternity testing Forensic DNA Chemical warfare. and from here it's my pleasure to invite everyone under or post graduates to join this group to work as a one group. Elharith Hamad Alrayah Group Admin 
                </div>

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hey Friends, Group exclusively for psychologists and students who are interested in Psychology Workshops, Seminars, Conferences, Webinars, Research opportunities, Fellowships, Scholarships, Internships and Jobs around the world. It is difficult for us to find information about opportunities for our professional development throughout the world. While these opportunities may be mentioned in other forums, they are sometimes difficult to find amongst all of the internet discussions. All members of this group are encouraged to post opportunities, whether they are the organizers, participants, or merely familiar with the opportunity. Opportunities might include any topic that would be of professional interest to psychologists. Please add your events, scholarship, internship, fellowships and job listings to our group. Remember, this group is for promoting psychology related study, events, and positions. It should not be used for other purposes. Our members are from around the world. Lets respect each one's culture and refrain ourselves from disturbing comments and posts. Follow our group to see the latest updates from our members as they happen around the world, and while you are here, don't forget to stop by our posts from Asia, Africa, America and Europe, the four corners of the world.. A good post can change your life… take you closer to your dreams… All the best…. Those who are not from Psychology Background, Pls refrain from joining.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Air Force Engineering &amp; Acquisition (62E/63A) Officer Assignments
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is the official page of the Engineering (62E) and Acquisition (63A) Officer Assignments Team (OAT). Our goal is to further transparency by disseminating assignment and force development related information to members of our career fields as quickly as possible while encouraging collaboration related to these topics. Rules of Engagement for posting: 1) Please be professional: what you say will be read by hundreds (if not thousands) of people, many of whom are senior leaders in your career field who may be stationed where you are. Keep this in mind when you address others on the site. 2) Add rank/AFSC to your posts: sign at least your first post to any new thread with your rank &amp; core AFSC (or retired core rank/AFSC). Our expectation is that this type of attribution will keep discourse on this page professional. If you forget, admins will gently remind you… but, if you just don’t follow the rules, we will amicably part ways. 3) Mutual respect: we're all in this together to create a welcoming, collaborative environment. Treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but mutual respect is required. 4) No hate speech or bullying: make sure everyone feels safe and respected. Bullying of any kind isn't allowed — no references to race, religion, culture, political affiliation, sexual orientation, gender, or identity. 5) No commercial/personal advertisement, promotions or spam: give more than you take from this group. Self-promotion, spam, and irrelevant links aren't allowed. 6) 62E/63A Assignments, Developmental Education, Force Development focus: Please limit posts and replies to these topics. 7) This is not a place to share your personal political perceptive or show disrespect for the chain of command. *Important* Please review the portal and Milsuite sites before posting a question (can't post FOUO on this site). There is a decent chance you can find the answer to your question there. For example, the DT Mentor Sheet found on Milsuite &amp; the portal site has a wealth of info like assignment cycle and Developmental Team (DT) timelines, the Non-Rated Prioritization Plan, Vector Points, Promo Board Schedules, AFPC phone numbers and more. You will also find the most recent AFPC Spread-the-Word briefs, AAD/SPEED info, and assignment cycle specifics like Hot Jobs. Milsuite: https://www.milsuite.mil/book/groups/air-force-engineering-acquisition-62e63a-officer-assignment-team-oat (note: there are known compatibility issues with Internet Explorer...try using Google Chrome instead and selecting your E-Mail certificate). Portal page: https://www.my.af.mil/gcss-af/USAF/ep/globalTab.do?channelPageId=sE3494DD04952199601495D8186C40180
                </div>
               </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Viktor E. Frankl - Logotherapy &amp; Existential Analysis
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Viktor Emil Frankl, M.D., Ph.D., (March 26, 1905 - September 2, 1997) was an Austrian neurologist and psychiatrist as well as a Holocaust survivor. Frankl was the founder of Logotherapy and Existential Analysis, the "Third Viennese School" of psychotherapy. His book, "Man's Search for Meaning" chronicles his experiences as a concentration camp inmate and describes his psychotherapeutic method of finding meaning in all forms of existence, even the most sordid ones, and thus a reason to continue living. He was one of the key figures in existential therapy. Viktor Frankl Institute of Vienna http://www.viktorfrankl.org/e/ Overview of accredited Institutes and Societies worldwide: http://www.viktorfrankl.org/php/instwwE.php Bio: http://logotherapy.univie.ac.at/e/lifeandwork.html Documentary 'Viktor and I': http://www.viktorandimovie.com Videos: http://logotherapy.univie.ac.at/e/audioE.html Books (in different languages): http://www.viktorfrankl.org/e/books_by_vf.html Quotes: http://thinkexist.com/quotes/viktor_frankl/ 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">7,046 位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">4 篇新帖</span></span>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Math Teachers Professional Learning Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for math teachers at all levels of instruction to discuss curriculum and best practices in their classrooms. This group should be a place where we can share ideas, concerns, and simply gather with other math teachers around the globe. Be aware that images shared in this group may be seen by a large number of people so please be sure you have permission to show student faces. If you do not, remember to edit the photo to remove faces. Do's: 1. Be kind to each other. We come from all different parts of the country and world and may have differing opinions at times. Be respectful of each other. 2. Ask questions. The responses from other math teachers are amazing and everyone learns from each other. 3. Share what's working in your classroom. 4. Reply to other teacher's where you can add value. What works in your class may likely work in someone else's. 5. Add your teacher friends! The more we have here, the more opportunities we have for collaboration. Be sure to tell them to answer the membership questions when you invite them. 5. Most of all, be positive! It can be so easy to be negative in the climate we work in, but this group is about helping and strengthening other teachers. Please DON'T: 1. Be inconsiderate, disrespectful or rude. 2. This group is not for promotion of your own products, including YouTube stations or TPT stores, unless they happen to add to an already ongoing discussion.
                </div>
               </div>
